12.1 WVM Resolution - MESA.pdf ↗

12.1 WEST VALLEY-MISSION COMMUNITY COLLEGES DISTRICT RESOLUTION 2304181 SUPPORTING SENATE BILL 444, MATHEMATICS, ENGINEERING, SCIENCE, AND ACHIEVEMENT (MESA) PROGRAM - Recommendation: The Board of Trustees adopt Resolution No. 2304181 supporting Senate Bill 444. This bill would encourage community colleges to develop and implement Mathematics, Engineering, Science, Achievement (MESA) programs directed at identifying students affected by social, economic, and educational disadvantages, increasing the number of eligible students served under MESA programs, and increasing student success in transferring and completing baccalaureate degree programs in science, technology, engineering, and mathematics. The bill would require the Board of Governors to adopt regulations for purposes of MESA programs and would require those regulations to be consistent with specified requirements.
